>>> from pyomo.environ import *
>>> m = ConcreteModel()
>>> m.x = Var(within=NonNegativeReals)
>>> m.c = Constraint(rule = lambda m: m.x <= 100)
>>> m.o = Objective(rule = lambda m: 100*m.x, sense=maximize)
>>> m.dual = Suffix(direction=Suffix.IMPORT)
>>> 
>>> i = m.create_instance()
WARNING: DEPRECATION WARNING: Cannot call Model.create_instance() on a concrete model.
>>> i = m
>>> 
>>> opt = SolverFactory("cplex", solver_io="nl")
>>> opt.options['mipgap'] = 0.01
>>> opt.options['display'] = 1
>>> opt.options['bardisplay'] = 1
>>> opt.options['mipdisplay'] = 2
>>> opt.options['primalopt'] = ""
>>> opt.options['advance'] = 2
